/**
 * 获取可选好友列表
 */
function getAvailableFriendsForGroup() {
    const friends = [];

    try {
        // 从MVU变量中获取好友
        const relationshipSource = getRelationshipDataSource(currentPhoneData);
        if (relationshipSource) {
            getRelationshipKeys(relationshipSource).forEach(studentKey => {
                const friend = relationshipSource[studentKey];
                if (!friend || typeof friend !== 'object') return;
                const basicInfo = friend.basic_info || {};
                const displayName = restoreEraText(basicInfo.name || studentKey);
                friends.push({
                    id: basicInfo.phone || `friend_${studentKey}`,
                    name: displayName,
                    identity: basicInfo.school ? restoreEraText(basicInfo.school) : '未知学校'
                });
            });
        }

        // 从聊天记录中提取好友
        const chatFriends = extractFriendsFromChat();
        chatFriends.forEach(chatFriend => {
            // 检查是否已存在
            const exists = friends.some(f => f.id === chatFriend.id || f.name === chatFriend.name);
            if (!exists) {
                friends.push({
                    id: chatFriend.id,
                    name: chatFriend.name,
                    identity: '聊天记录'
                });
            }
        });

    } catch (error) {
    }

    return friends;
}

/**
 * 生成好友选择列表
 */
function generateFriendsSelectionList(friends) {
    return friends.map(friend => `
        <div class="friend-selection-item" data-friend-id="${friend.id}" data-friend-name="${friend.name}"
            style="display: flex; align-items: center; padding: 8px; margin-bottom: 4px; border-radius: 6px; cursor: pointer; transition: all 0.2s;"
            onmouseover="this.style.background='#f3f4f6'" onmouseout="this.style.background='transparent'">
            <input type="checkbox" class="friend-checkbox" value="${friend.id}" 
                style="margin-right: 10px; width: 16px; height: 16px; cursor: pointer;">
            <div style="flex: 1;">
                <div style="font-size: 13px; font-weight: 500; color: #1f2937;">${friend.name}</div>
                <div style="font-size: 11px; color: #9ca3af; margin-top: 2px;">${friend.identity}</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `).join('');
}

/**
 * 绑定创建群聊相关事件
 */
function bindCreateGroupEvents() {
    // 全选按钮
    $('#select-all-friends-btn').off('click').on('click', function () {
        const $checkboxes = $('.friend-checkbox');
        const allChecked = $checkboxes.toArray().every(cb => cb.checked);

        $checkboxes.prop('checked', !allChecked);
        $(this).text(allChecked ? '全选' : '取消全选');

        // 更新已选成员显示
        updateSelectedMembers();
    });

    // 好友选择
    $('.friend-checkbox').off('change').on('change', function () {
        updateSelectedMembers();
    });

    // 创建按钮
    $('#create-group-submit-btn').off('click').on('click', function () {
        createGroup();
    });

    //  移除成员按钮（使用事件委托）
    $('body').off('click.removeMember').on('click.removeMember', '.remove-member-btn', function (e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
        const friendId = $(this).data('friend-id');
        removeMember(friendId);
    });
}

/**
 * 更新已选成员显示
 */
function updateSelectedMembers() {
    const $container = $('#selected-members-container');
    const $checkboxes = $('.friend-checkbox:checked');

    // 保留"我"标签
    $container.html(`
        <div class="selected-member-tag" data-member="我" style="display: inline-flex; align-items: center; padding: 6px 12px; background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%); color: white; border-radius: 16px; font-size: 13px; font-weight: 500;">
            <span>我 (群主)</span>
        </div>
    `);

    // 添加选中的好友
    $checkboxes.each(function () {
        const $item = $(this).closest('.friend-selection-item');
        const friendName = $item.data('friend-name');
        const friendId = $item.data('friend-id');

        $container.append(`
            <div class="selected-member-tag" data-member="${friendId}" style="display: inline-flex; align-items: center; padding: 6px 12px; background: #3b82f6; color: white; border-radius: 16px; font-size: 13px; font-weight: 500;">
                <span>${friendName}</span>
                <span class="remove-member-btn" data-friend-id="${friendId}" style="margin-left: 6px; cursor: pointer; opacity: 0.8;">✕</span>
            </div>
        `);
    });
}

/**
 * 移除已选成员
 */
function removeMember(friendId) {
    $(`.friend-checkbox[value="${friendId}"]`).prop('checked', false);

    // 更新显示
    updateSelectedMembers();
}

/**
 * 创建群聊
 */
async function createGroup() {
    const groupName = $('#group-name-input').val().trim();
    const groupId = $('#group-id-input').val().trim();
    const $checkboxes = $('.friend-checkbox:checked');

    // 验证输入
    if (!groupName) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error('请输入群聊名称');
        }
        return;
    }

    if (!groupId || !/^\d+$/.test(groupId)) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error('请输入有效的群聊ID（纯数字）');
        }
        return;
    }

    if ($checkboxes.length === 0) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error('请至少选择一个群成员');
        }
        return;
    }

    // 收集成员列表
    const members = ['我']; // 群主默认在群里
    $checkboxes.each(function () {
        const $item = $(this).closest('.friend-selection-item');
        const friendName = $item.data('friend-name');
        members.push(friendName);
    });

    // 格式化群聊信息: [群聊|群名|群ID|成员列表]
    const membersStr = members.join('、');
    const groupInfo = `[群聊|${groupName}|${groupId}|${membersStr}]`;


    try {

        // 检查 SillyTavern 是否准备就绪
        const targetWindow = window.parent || window;
        if (!targetWindow.SillyTavern || typeof targetWindow.SillyTavern.getContext !== 'function') {
            throw new Error('SillyTavern API 不可用');
        }

        const context = targetWindow.SillyTavern.getContext();
        if (!context || !context.chat || !Array.isArray(context.chat)) {
            throw new Error('聊天上下文不可用');
        }


        // 构建消息对象（参考 mobile-master/context-editor.js 的 addMessage 方法）
        const message = {
            name: '系统',
            is_user: true,
            is_system: false,
            force_avatar: false,
            mes: groupInfo,
            send_date: Date.now(),
            extra: {}
        };

        // 添加到聊天数组
        context.chat.push(message);

        // 使用 SillyTavern API 添加消息
        if (typeof context.addOneMessage === 'function') {
            context.addOneMessage(message);
        }

        // 保存聊天
        if (typeof context.saveChat === 'function') {
            await context.saveChat();
        }


        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.success(`群聊 "${groupName}" 创建成功！已添加到聊天记录`);
        }

        // 延迟关闭面板并刷新列表
        setTimeout(() => {
            closeAppPanel();
            // 刷新消息列表
            if (currentPhoneData) {
                const content = generateMessagesPanel(currentPhoneData);
                $('#phone-app-body').html(content);
            }
        }, 1000);

    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error('创建群聊失败: ' + error.message);
        }
    }
}

function getDefaultStoryCompletedChapters() {
    return BA_STORY_VOLUMES.reduce((acc, vol) => {
        acc[vol] = [];
        return acc;
    }, {});
}

function normalizeStoryBoolean(value, defaultValue = true) {
    if (typeof value === 'boolean') return value;
    if (typeof value === 'number') return value !== 0;
    if (typeof value === 'string') {
        const normalized = value.trim().toLowerCase();
        if (['true', '1', 'yes', 'y', '是'].includes(normalized)) return true;
        if (['false', '0', 'no', 'n', '否', ''].includes(normalized)) return false;
    }
    return defaultValue;
}

function ensureStoryManagerStructure(gameData) {
    if (!gameData.story_manager || typeof gameData.story_manager !== 'object') {
        gameData.story_manager = {};
    }

    const storyManager = gameData.story_manager;
    debugStoryChapterLog('ensureStoryManagerStructure 归一化前', snapshotStoryManager(gameData));
    storyManager.enabled = normalizeStoryBoolean(storyManager.enabled, true);
    storyManager.mode = storyManager.mode === '特殊' ? '特殊' : '日常';

    if (!storyManager.current || typeof storyManager.current !== 'object') {
        storyManager.current = {};
    }
    storyManager.current.vol = typeof storyManager.current.vol === 'string' ? storyManager.current.vol : '';
    storyManager.current.chapter = typeof storyManager.current.chapter === 'string' ? storyManager.current.chapter : '';
    storyManager.current.seq = Math.max(0, Math.floor(Number(storyManager.current.seq) || 0));

    if (!storyManager.completed_chapters || typeof storyManager.completed_chapters !== 'object') {
        storyManager.completed_chapters = {};
    }
    const defaults = getDefaultStoryCompletedChapters();
    BA_STORY_VOLUMES.forEach(vol => {
        const chapters = Array.isArray(storyManager.completed_chapters[vol])
            ? storyManager.completed_chapters[vol]
            : defaults[vol];
        const allowed = (BA_STORY_CHAPTERS[vol] || []).map(item => item.id);
        storyManager.completed_chapters[vol] = _.uniq(chapters.filter(ch => allowed.includes(ch)));
    });

    debugStoryChapterLog('ensureStoryManagerStructure 归一化后', snapshotStoryManager(gameData));
    return storyManager;
}

function getStoryChapterMeta(vol, chapter) {
    return (BA_STORY_CHAPTERS[vol] || []).find(item => item.id === chapter) || null;
}

function getStoryEntryName(vol, chapter) {
    return `${vol}${chapter}`;
}

function getStoryVolumeDisplayName(vol) {
    return escapeHtml(restoreEraText(vol || ''));
}

function getStoryChapterDisplayName(vol, chapter) {
    const meta = getStoryChapterMeta(vol, chapter);
    if (!meta) return `${chapter}`;
    return meta.title ? `${chapter} · ${escapeHtml(restoreEraText(meta.title))}` : chapter;
}

function getPreviousStoryChapters(vol, chapter) {
    const chapters = (BA_STORY_CHAPTERS[vol] || []).map(item => item.id);
    const index = chapters.indexOf(chapter);
    if (index <= 0) return [];
    return chapters.slice(0, index);
}

function getStoryWorldbookNames() {
    if (storyWorldbookNamesCache) return storyWorldbookNamesCache;
    if (typeof getCharWorldbookNames !== 'function') return [];

    const charWorldbooks = getCharWorldbookNames('current') || {};
    storyWorldbookNamesCache = _.uniq([
        charWorldbooks.primary,
        ...(Array.isArray(charWorldbooks.additional) ? charWorldbooks.additional : [])
    ].filter(Boolean));

    return storyWorldbookNamesCache;
}

function getStoryWorldbookActiveEntry(storyManager) {
    if (!storyManager || storyManager.enabled === false) return null;
    if (storyManager.mode !== '特殊') return null;

    const vol = storyManager.current?.vol || '';
    const chapter = storyManager.current?.chapter || '';
    if (!vol || !chapter) return null;

    const entryName = getStoryEntryName(vol, chapter);
    return BA_STORY_ENTRY_SET.has(entryName) ? entryName : null;
}

async function syncStoryWorldbookEntriesDirectly(storyManager) {
    try {
        if (typeof updateWorldbookWith !== 'function') return;

        const worldbookNames = getStoryWorldbookNames();
        if (!worldbookNames.length) return;

        const activeEntry = getStoryWorldbookActiveEntry(storyManager);

        for (const worldbookName of worldbookNames) {
            await updateWorldbookWith(worldbookName, worldbook => worldbook.map(entry => {
                if (!BA_STORY_ENTRY_SET.has(entry.name)) return entry;

                const shouldEnable = !!activeEntry && entry.name === activeEntry;
                if (entry.enabled === shouldEnable) return entry;

                return { ...entry, enabled: shouldEnable };
            }));
        }

        debugStoryChapterLog('syncStoryWorldbookEntriesDirectly 完成', {
            activeEntry,
            worldbookNames
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.warn('[碧蓝档案小手机] 剧情世界书直接同步失败:', error);
    }
}

function syncStoryChapterSelection(storyManager) {
    const currentVol = storyManager?.current?.vol;
    const currentChapter = storyManager?.current?.chapter;
    const fallbackVol = currentVol && BA_STORY_CHAPTERS[currentVol] ? currentVol : storyChapterUiState.selectedVol;
    const safeVol = BA_STORY_CHAPTERS[fallbackVol] ? fallbackVol : BA_STORY_VOLUMES[0];
    const chapterOptions = BA_STORY_CHAPTERS[safeVol] || [];
    const preferredChapter = safeVol === currentVol && currentChapter
        ? currentChapter
        : storyChapterUiState.selectedChapter;
    const safeChapter = chapterOptions.some(item => item.id === preferredChapter)
        ? preferredChapter
        : (chapterOptions[0]?.id || 'Ch1');

    storyChapterUiState.selectedVol = safeVol;
    storyChapterUiState.selectedChapter = safeChapter;
}

function formatStoryCompletedList(chapters) {
    if (!Array.isArray(chapters) || chapters.length === 0) return '无';
    return chapters.join('、');
}

function generateStoryChapterManagerPanel(data) {
    const storyManager = ensureStoryManagerStructure(_.cloneDeep(data || {}));
    syncStoryChapterSelection(storyManager);

    const isPaused = storyManager.enabled === false;
    const selectedVol = storyChapterUiState.selectedVol;
    const selectedChapter = storyChapterUiState.selectedChapter;
    const selectedEntryName = getStoryEntryName(selectedVol, selectedChapter);
    const currentVol = storyManager.current?.vol || '';
    const currentChapter = storyManager.current?.chapter || '';
    const currentSeq = Number(storyManager.current?.seq) || 0;
    const currentEntryName = currentVol && currentChapter ? getStoryEntryName(currentVol, currentChapter) : '无';
    const completedForSelectedVol = storyManager.completed_chapters?.[selectedVol] || [];

    const volumeButtons = BA_STORY_VOLUMES.map(vol => {
        const active = vol === selectedVol;
        return `
            <button class="story-volume-btn" data-vol="${vol}"
                style="padding: 8px 12px; border: none; border-radius: 999px; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 700; cursor: pointer; transition: all 0.15s ease;
                ${active
                    ? 'background: linear-gradient(135deg, #06b6d4 0%, #0891b2 100%); color: white; box-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(8,145,178,0.35);'
                    : 'background: #e5e7eb; color: #374151;'}">
                ${getStoryVolumeDisplayName(vol)}
            </button>
        `;
    }).join('');

    const chapterButtons = (BA_STORY_CHAPTERS[selectedVol] || []).map(item => {
        const chapterId = item.id;
        const isSelected = chapterId === selectedChapter;
        const isCompleted = completedForSelectedVol.includes(chapterId);
        const isCurrent = currentVol === selectedVol && currentChapter === chapterId && storyManager.mode === '特殊';
        let style = 'background: #f3f4f6; color: #1f2937; border: 1px solid #e5e7eb;';

        if (isSelected) {
            style = 'background: linear-gradient(135deg, #2563eb 0%, #1d4ed8 100%); color: white; border: 1px solid transparent; box-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(37,99,235,0.35);';
        } else if (isCurrent) {
            style = 'background: linear-gradient(135deg, #10b981 0%, #059669 100%); color: white; border: 1px solid transparent;';
        } else if (isCompleted) {
            style = 'background: #ecfdf5; color: #047857; border: 1px solid #a7f3d0;';
        }

        return `
            <button class="story-chapter-btn" data-vol="${selectedVol}" data-chapter="${chapterId}"
                style="width: 100%; text-align: left; padding: 12px 14px; border-radius: 12px; cursor: pointer; transition: all 0.15s ease; ${style}">
                <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; gap: 10px;">
                    <div style="font-size: 13px; font-weight: 700;">${chapterId}</div>
                    <div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.9; white-space: nowrap;">
                        ${isSelected ? '已选中' : isCurrent ? '进行中' : isCompleted ? '已完成' : '未完成'}
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div style="font-size: 11px; margin-top: 6px; line-height: 1.5; opacity: 0.95;">
                    ${escapeHtml(restoreEraText(item.title))}
                </div>
            </button>
        `;
    }).join('');

    const completedSummary = BA_STORY_VOLUMES.map(vol => {
        const completed = storyManager.completed_chapters?.[vol] || [];
        return `
            <div style="padding: 10px 12px; background: #f9fafb; border-radius: 10px; border: 1px solid #e5e7eb;">
                <div style="font-size: 12px; font-weight: 700; color: #374151; margin-bottom: 4px;">${getStoryVolumeDisplayName(vol)}</div>
                <div style="font-size: 11px; color: #6b7280; line-height: 1.6;">${escapeHtml(formatStoryCompletedList(completed))}</div>
            </div>
        `;
    }).join('');

    return `
        <div class="list-item" style="margin-bottom: 16px; ${isPaused ? 'background: linear-gradient(135deg, #ef4444 0%, #dc2626 100%); border: 3px solid #fbbf24; animation: pausePulse 1.5s ease-in-out infinite;' : ''}">
            <div class="list-item-header">
                <span class="list-item-name" style="${isPaused ? 'color: white;' : ''}">⏸️ 剧情控制</span>
                ${isPaused ? '<span style="background: #fbbf24; color: #1f2937; padding: 2px 8px; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 11px; font-weight: 700;">已暂停</span>' : ''}
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top: 12px;">
                <button class="story-pause-btn"
                    style="width: 100%; padding: 14px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; font-size: 15px; font-weight: 700; cursor: pointer; transition: all 0.15s ease;
                    ${isPaused
                        ? 'background: linear-gradient(135deg, #22c55e 0%, #16a34a 100%); color: white; box-shadow: 0 4px 15px rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.4);'
                        : 'background: linear-gradient(135deg, #f97316 0%, #ea580c 100%); color: white;'}">
                    <i class="fas ${isPaused ? 'fa-play' : 'fa-pause'}" style="margin-right: 8px;"></i>${isPaused ? '恢复剧情' : '暂停剧情'}
                </button>
            </div>
            ${isPaused ? '<div style="margin-top: 10px; padding: 10px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.15); border-radius: 6px; font-size: 12px; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.9); text-align: center;">⚠️ 剧情已暂停，主线章节世界书会保持关闭，想跑剧情别忘了恢复哦！</div>' : ''}
        </div>

        <div class="list-item" style="background: linear-gradient(135deg, #06b6d4 0%, #0f766e 100%); color: white; margin-bottom: 16px;">
            <div style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 12px;">
                <i class="fas fa-book-open" style="font-size: 30px; margin-bottom: 8px;"></i>
                <div style="font-size: 18px; font-weight: 700;">剧情章节管理</div>
            </div>
            <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(2, 1fr); gap: 10px;">
                <div style="text-align: center; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.18); padding: 12px; border-radius: 10px;">
                    <div style="font-size: 14px; font-weight: 700;">${escapeHtml(storyManager.mode || '日常')}</div>
                    <div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.9; margin-top: 4px;">当前模式</div>
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: center; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.18); padding: 12px; border-radius: 10px;">
                    <div style="font-size: 14px; font-weight: 700;">Seq ${currentSeq || 0}</div>
                    <div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.9; margin-top: 4px;">当前小节</div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top: 12px; padding: 10px 12px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.18); border-radius: 10px; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.6;">
                <div>当前章节：${escapeHtml(currentEntryName)}</div>
                <div>选中章节：${escapeHtml(selectedEntryName)}</div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="list-item" style="margin-bottom: 16px;">
            <div class="list-item-header">
                <span class="list-item-name">📚 选择卷目</span>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top: 12px; display: flex; flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 8px;">
                ${volumeButtons}
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="list-item" style="margin-bottom: 16px;">
            <div class="list-item-header">
                <span class="list-item-name">🧭 选择章节</span>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top: 12px; display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 10px;">
                ${chapterButtons}
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top: 12px; padding: 10px 12px; background: #f9fafb; border-radius: 8px; font-size: 11px; color: #6b7280; line-height: 1.7;">
                进入章节后会将剧情切到 <strong>${escapeHtml(selectedEntryName)}</strong> 的 <strong>seq:1</strong>，并将当前卷已完成记录更新为：${escapeHtml(formatStoryCompletedList(getPreviousStoryChapters(selectedVol, selectedChapter)))}
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top: 12px;">
                <button class="story-enter-btn"
                    style="width: 100%; padding: 14px; border: none; border-radius: 10px; font-size: 15px; font-weight: 700; cursor: pointer; color: white; background: linear-gradient(135deg, #2563eb 0%, #1d4ed8 100%); box-shadow: 0 4px 15px rgba(37,99,235,0.35);">
                    <i class="fas fa-play-circle" style="margin-right: 8px;"></i>从头进入 ${escapeHtml(selectedEntryName)}
                </button>
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="list-item">
            <div class="list-item-header">
                <span class="list-item-name">✅ 已完成章节</span>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top: 12px; display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 8px;">
                ${completedSummary}
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
}

function bindStoryChapterManagerEvents() {
    const $appBody = $('#phone-app-body');
    if ($appBody.length === 0) return;

    $appBody.off('click.storychapter');

    $appBody.on('click.storychapter', '.story-volume-btn', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        const vol = $(this).data('vol');
        if (!BA_STORY_CHAPTERS[vol]) return;

        storyChapterUiState.selectedVol = vol;
        storyChapterUiState.selectedChapter = BA_STORY_CHAPTERS[vol][0]?.id || 'Ch1';
        refreshStoryChapterManagerPanel();
    });

    $appBody.on('click.storychapter', '.story-chapter-btn', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        const vol = $(this).data('vol');
        const chapter = $(this).data('chapter');
        if (!vol || !chapter) return;

        storyChapterUiState.selectedVol = vol;
        storyChapterUiState.selectedChapter = chapter;
        refreshStoryChapterManagerPanel();
    });

    $appBody.on('click.storychapter', '.story-pause-btn', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        handleStoryChapterPauseToggle();
    });

    $appBody.on('click.storychapter', '.story-enter-btn', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        handleStoryChapterEnter();
    });
}

function refreshStoryChapterManagerPanel(dataOverride = null, options = {}) {
    try {
        const { skipFetch = false } = options;

        if (dataOverride && typeof dataOverride === 'object') {
            currentPhoneData = dataOverride;
            window.mvuGameData = dataOverride;
        } else if (!skipFetch) {
            fetchLatestMvuData(true);
        }

        debugStoryChapterLog('refreshStoryChapterManagerPanel 使用的数据', snapshotStoryManager(currentPhoneData));
        updateStoryChapterPauseBadge(currentPhoneData);

        if (currentPanel !== 'chapter') return;

        const content = generateStoryChapterManagerPanel(currentPhoneData || {});
        $('#phone-app-body').html(content);
        bindStoryChapterManagerEvents();
    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error(`刷新剧情章节面板失败: ${error.message}`, '错误');
        }
    }
}

async function handleStoryChapterPauseToggle() {
    try {
        const mvuData = fetchRawMvuData();
        const gameData = extractMvuGameData(mvuData);
        const storyManager = ensureStoryManagerStructure(gameData);
        const currentlyPaused = storyManager.enabled === false;
        debugStoryChapterLog('handleStoryChapterPauseToggle 点击前', {
            currentlyPaused,
            storyManager: snapshotStoryManager(gameData)
        });

        // currentlyPaused 表示“当前是否已暂停”，而 enabled 表示“是否启用”
        // 所以切换时应当写入相反的 enabled 状态：
        // 已暂停 -> enabled = true
        // 未暂停 -> enabled = false
        storyManager.enabled = currentlyPaused;
        debugStoryChapterLog('handleStoryChapterPauseToggle 写入前', snapshotStoryManager(gameData));

        applyGameDataToMvuContainer(mvuData, gameData);
        await persistMvuGameData(mvuData);
        debugStoryChapterLog('handleStoryChapterPauseToggle replaceMvuData 已提交', snapshotStoryManager(gameData));

        await syncStoryWorldbookEntriesDirectly(storyManager);
        notifyStoryManagerSync(gameData);
        currentPhoneData = gameData;
        window.mvuGameData = gameData;
        updatePhoneData(gameData);
        refreshStoryChapterManagerPanel(gameData, { skipFetch: true });

        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr[currentlyPaused ? 'success' : 'warning'](
                currentlyPaused ? '剧情章节管理已恢复' : '剧情章节管理已暂停',
                '剧情章节管理'
            );
        }
    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error(`切换剧情暂停失败: ${error.message}`, '错误');
        }
    }
}

async function handleStoryChapterEnter() {
    const selectedVol = storyChapterUiState.selectedVol;
    const selectedChapter = storyChapterUiState.selectedChapter;
    const entryName = getStoryEntryName(selectedVol, selectedChapter);
    const previousCompleted = getPreviousStoryChapters(selectedVol, selectedChapter);
    const chapterLabel = getStoryChapterDisplayName(selectedVol, selectedChapter);

    const confirmed = await showCustomConfirm({
        title: `进入 ${entryName}`,
        icon: '📖',
        message: `确定要从头开始进入 ${entryName} 吗？<br><br>将切换到该章节的 seq:1，并把 ${selectedVol} 的已完成记录设置为：${escapeHtml(formatStoryCompletedList(previousCompleted))}`,
        confirmText: '进入剧情',
        cancelText: '取消',
        itemInfo: {
            icon: '📝',
            name: entryName,
            description: chapterLabel
        }
    });

    if (!confirmed) return;

    try {
        const mvuData = fetchRawMvuData();
        const gameData = extractMvuGameData(mvuData);
        const storyManager = ensureStoryManagerStructure(gameData);
        debugStoryChapterLog('handleStoryChapterEnter 进入前', snapshotStoryManager(gameData));

        storyManager.enabled = true;
        storyManager.mode = '特殊';
        storyManager.current.vol = selectedVol;
        storyManager.current.chapter = selectedChapter;
        storyManager.current.seq = 1;
        storyManager.completed_chapters[selectedVol] = previousCompleted;
        debugStoryChapterLog('handleStoryChapterEnter 写入前', snapshotStoryManager(gameData));

        applyGameDataToMvuContainer(mvuData, gameData);
        await persistMvuGameData(mvuData);
        debugStoryChapterLog('handleStoryChapterEnter replaceMvuData 已提交', snapshotStoryManager(gameData));

        await syncStoryWorldbookEntriesDirectly(storyManager);
        notifyStoryManagerSync(gameData);
        currentPhoneData = gameData;
        window.mvuGameData = gameData;
        updatePhoneData(gameData);
        refreshStoryChapterManagerPanel(gameData, { skipFetch: true });

        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.success(`已进入 ${entryName} · seq 1`, '剧情章节管理');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error(`进入章节失败: ${error.message}`, '错误');
        }
        return;
    }

    try {
        const message = `前往处理${entryName}剧情，请按大纲推进进入 seq:1 的场景`;
        if (!window.messageSender) {
            throw new Error('消息发送器未初始化');
        }

        const success = await window.messageSender.sendToChat(message);
        if (success) {
            if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
                toastr.success(`消息已发送：${message}`, '剧情章节管理');
            }
        } else {
            throw new Error('发送失败');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error(`章节已切换，但发送消息失败: ${error.message}`, '提示');
        }
    }
}

function updateStoryChapterPauseBadge(dataSource = null) {
    try {
        const storyManager = dataSource?.story_manager || currentPhoneData?.story_manager;
        const isPaused = storyManager?.enabled === false;
        const $badge = $('.chapter-pause-badge');
        debugStoryChapterLog('updateStoryChapterPauseBadge 判定', {
            storyManager: storyManager ? {
                enabled: storyManager.enabled,
                enabledType: typeof storyManager.enabled,
                mode: storyManager.mode,
                current: _.cloneDeep(storyManager.current || {})
            } : null,
            isPaused,
            badgeCount: $badge.length
        });

        if (isPaused) {
            $badge.show();
        } else {
            $badge.hide();
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.warn('[碧蓝档案小手机] 更新剧情暂停红点失败:', error);
    }
}

/**
 * 自定义确认弹窗
 * @param {Object} options - 弹窗配置
 * @param {string} options.title - 标题
 * @param {string} options.message - 消息内容
 * @param {string} options.icon - 图标emoji
 * @param {Object} options.itemInfo - 商品详细信息（可选）
 * @param {string} options.confirmText - 确认按钮文字
 * @param {string} options.cancelText - 取消按钮文字
 * @returns {Promise<boolean>} - 用户选择结果
 */
function showCustomConfirm(options = {}) {

    return new Promise((resolve) => {
        const {
            title = '确认操作',
            message = '确定要继续吗？',
            icon = '❓',
            itemInfo = null,
            confirmText = '确认',
            cancelText = '取消'
        } = options;


        // 构建商品信息HTML（带内联样式）
        let itemInfoHtml = '';
        if (itemInfo) {
            itemInfoHtml = `
                <div class="confirm-item-info" style="background:rgba(102,126,234,0.1);border:1px solid rgba(102,126,234,0.3);border-radius:12px;padding:16px;margin-bottom:24px;display:block;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;">
                    <div class="confirm-item-name" style="display:block;width:100%;margin-bottom:8px;font-size:16px;font-weight:600;color:#f3f4f6;">
                        <span style="margin-right:8px;">${itemInfo.icon || '🎁'}</span>
                        <span>${itemInfo.name || '未知物品'}</span>
                    </div>
                    ${itemInfo.description ? `<div class="confirm-item-desc" style="display:block;width:100%;margin-bottom:8px;font-size:14px;color:#d1d5db;line-height:1.6;">${itemInfo.description}</div>` : ''}
                    ${itemInfo.price !== undefined ? `
                        <div class="confirm-item-price" style="display:block;width:100%;margin-bottom:0;font-size:15px;color:#fbbf24;font-weight:600;">
                            <span>💰 价格：</span>
                            <span>${itemInfo.price} 任务代币</span>
                        </div>
                    ` : ''}
                </div>
            `;
        }

        //  计算弹窗宽度
        const windowWidth = $(window).width();
        const bodyWidth = $('body').width();
        const containerWidth = windowWidth || bodyWidth || 400;
        let modalWidth = Math.min(Math.max(containerWidth * 0.9, 300), 480);
        if (modalWidth < 300 || isNaN(modalWidth)) {
            modalWidth = 400;
        }

        // 创建弹窗HTML（直接在HTML中设置内联样式）
        const confirmHtml = `
            <div class="custom-confirm-overlay" style="position:fixed;top:0;left:0;right:0;bottom:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.5);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;z-index:100000;opacity:0;transition:opacity 0.3s ease-out;">
                <div class="custom-confirm-modal" style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,#667eea 0%,#764ba2 100%);border-radius:20px;padding:2px;width:${modalWidth}px;max-width:480px;min-width:300px;box-shadow:0 12px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.4);transform:translateY(30px) scale(0.95);opacity:0;transition:all 0.3s ease-out;display:block;box-sizing:border-box;margin:0 auto;">
                    <div class="custom-confirm-content" style="background:#1f2937;border-radius:18px;padding:28px 24px 20px;display:block;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;min-height:100px;">
                        <div class="confirm-icon" style="width:64px;height:64px;margin:0 auto 20px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#667eea 0%,#764ba2 100%);border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:32px;">${icon}</div>
                        <div class="confirm-title" style="font-size:22px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:16px;color:#f3f4f6;text-align:center;display:block;width:100%;">${title}</div>
                        <div class="confirm-message" style="font-size:15px;line-height:1.7;color:#d1d5db;margin-bottom:24px;text-align:center;display:block;width:100%;">${message}</div>
                        ${itemInfoHtml}
                        <div class="confirm-buttons" style="display:flex;gap:12px;width:100%;">
                            <button class="confirm-btn confirm-btn-cancel" data-action="cancel" style="flex:1;padding:14px 20px;border:none;border-radius:12px;font-size:15px;font-weight:600;cursor:pointer;background:#374151;color:#d1d5db;min-height:48px;">
                                ${cancelText}
                            </button>
                            <button class="confirm-btn confirm-btn-confirm" data-action="confirm" style="flex:1;padding:14px 20px;border:none;border-radius:12px;font-size:15px;font-weight:600;cursor:pointer;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#667eea 0%,#764ba2 100%);color:white;min-height:48px;">
                                ${confirmText}
                            </button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        // 创建弹窗元素
        const $confirm = $(confirmHtml);

        //  添加到父窗口的 body（而不是 iframe 内），这样即使手机关闭弹窗仍可见
        const targetBody = (window.parent !== window) ? $(window.parent.document.body) : $('body');
        $confirm.appendTo(targetBody);

        // 获取modal和content元素
        const $modal = $confirm.find('.custom-confirm-modal');
        const $content = $confirm.find('.custom-confirm-content');

        //  强制触发重绘
        $confirm[0].offsetHeight;

        // 检查尺寸
        const confirmRect = $confirm[0].getBoundingClientRect();
        const modalRect = $modal[0].getBoundingClientRect();

        // 渐入动画
        setTimeout(() => {
            $confirm.css('opacity', '1');
        }, 10);

        // 弹窗上滑动画
        setTimeout(() => {
            $modal.css({
                'transform': 'translateY(0) scale(1)',
                'opacity': '1'
            });
        }, 50);

        // 处理按钮点击
        const handleChoice = (confirmed) => {

            $confirm.fadeOut(200, () => {
                $confirm.remove();
                resolve(confirmed);
            });
        };

        // 绑定事件
        $confirm.find('[data-action="confirm"]').on('click', () => handleChoice(true));
        $confirm.find('[data-action="cancel"]').on('click', () => handleChoice(false));

        // 点击遮罩层取消
        $confirm.on('click', (e) => {
            if ($(e.target).hasClass('custom-confirm-overlay')) {
                handleChoice(false);
            }
        });

        // ESC键取消
        const handleEsc = (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                $(document).off('keydown', handleEsc);
                handleChoice(false);
            }
        };
        $(document).on('keydown', handleEsc);

        // Enter键确认
        const handleEnter = (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                $(document).off('keydown', handleEnter);
                handleChoice(true);
            }
        };
        $(document).on('keydown', handleEnter);

        // 自动聚焦确认按钮
        setTimeout(() => {
            $confirm.find('.confirm-btn-confirm').focus();
        }, 100);
    });
}

// ==================== 队伍管理相关函数 ====================

/**
 * 显示学生选择器（iframe内实现）
 */
function showStudentSelector() {

    const relationshipSource = getRelationshipDataSource(currentPhoneData);
    if (!relationshipSource) {
        return;
    }

    // 获取所有未在队伍中的学生
    const availableStudents = [];
    getRelationshipKeys(relationshipSource).forEach(studentKey => {
        const student = relationshipSource[studentKey];
        if (!student || typeof student !== 'object') return;

        const basicInfo = student.basic_info || {};
        if (basicInfo.is_in_team !== true) {
            availableStudents.push({ studentKey, student });
        }
    });


    if (availableStudents.length === 0) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.info('没有可添加的学生，所有学生都已在队伍中');
        }
        return;
    }

    // 生成学生选择列表
    let html = `
        <div style="padding: 12px; background: linear-gradient(135deg, #10b981 0%, #059669 100%); color: white; border-radius: 8px; margin-bottom: 16px;">
            <div style="font-weight: 600; font-size: 14px;">📋 选择学生加入队伍</div>
            <div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.9; margin-top: 4px;">可用学生: ${availableStudents.length}人</div>
        </div>
        <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fill, minmax(180px, 1fr)); gap: 12px;">
    `;

    availableStudents.forEach(({ studentKey, student }) => {
        const basicInfo = student.basic_info || {};
        const relationship = student.relationship || {};
        const displayName = escapeHtml(basicInfo.name || studentKey);
        const schoolLabel = escapeHtml(normalizeSchoolName(basicInfo.school || '未知学校'));
        const affection = relationship.affection ?? 0;

        html += `
            <div class="selector-student-card" data-student-key="${escapeHtml(studentKey)}" 
                 style="cursor: pointer; border: 1px solid #e5e7eb; border-radius: 8px; padding: 12px; transition: all 0.2s; background: white;">
                <div style="font-weight: 600; font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 4px; color: #2563eb;">${displayName}</div>
                <div style="font-size: 11px; color: #6b7280; margin-bottom: 6px;">${schoolLabel}</div>
                <div style="font-size: 11px; color: #ec4899;">❤ ${affection}</div>
            </div>
        `;
    });

    html += '</div>';

    // 在当前面板显示学生选择器
    const $appBody = $('#phone-app-body');
    const currentContent = $appBody.html();

    // 保存当前内容以便返回
    $appBody.data('previous-content', currentContent);

    $appBody.html(`
        <div style="padding: 12px;">
            <button id="back-to-team" style="margin-bottom: 12px; padding: 8px 16px; background: #6b7280; color: white; border: none; border-radius: 6px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 13px; font-weight: 600;">
                ← 返回队伍
            </button>
            ${html}
        </div>
    `);

    // 绑定返回按钮
    $('#back-to-team').on('click', function () {
        const previousContent = $appBody.data('previous-content');
        if (previousContent) {
            $appBody.html(previousContent);
        } else {
            // 如果没有保存的内容，重新生成队伍面板
            const content = generateTeamPanel(currentPhoneData);
            $appBody.html(content);
        }
    });

    // 绑定学生卡片点击
    $('.selector-student-card').on('click', function () {
        const studentKey = $(this).data('student-key');
        addStudentToTeam(studentKey);
    });
}

/**
 * 添加学生到队伍
 */
async function addStudentToTeam(studentKey) {

    try {
        const mvuData = fetchRawMvuData();
        const gameData = extractMvuGameData(mvuData);
        const relationshipStudents = gameData.relationship_students || {};

        if (!relationshipStudents[studentKey]) {
            throw new Error('找不到学生数据');
        }

        // 检查队伍是否已满
        let teamCount = 0;
        Object.keys(relationshipStudents).forEach(key => {
            if (relationshipStudents[key]?.basic_info?.is_in_team === true) {
                teamCount++;
            }
        });

        if (teamCount >= 4) {
            if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
                toastr.warning('队伍已满（最多4人）');
            }
            return;
        }

        //  直接修改数据
        if (!relationshipStudents[studentKey].basic_info) {
            relationshipStudents[studentKey].basic_info = {};
        }
        relationshipStudents[studentKey].basic_info.is_in_team = true;


        applyGameDataToMvuContainer(mvuData, gameData);
        await persistMvuGameData(mvuData);

        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.success('学生已加入队伍');
        }

        currentPhoneData = gameData;
        window.mvuGameData = gameData;
        const content = generateTeamPanel(gameData);
        $('#phone-app-body').html(content);
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                loadTeamStudentImages();
            });
        });

    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error('添加失败: ' + error.message);
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 从队伍中移除学生
 */
async function removeStudentFromTeam(studentKey) {

    try {
        const mvuData = fetchRawMvuData();
        const gameData = extractMvuGameData(mvuData);
        const relationshipStudents = gameData.relationship_students || {};

        if (!relationshipStudents[studentKey]) {
            throw new Error('找不到学生数据');
        }

        //  直接修改数据
        if (!relationshipStudents[studentKey].basic_info) {
            relationshipStudents[studentKey].basic_info = {};
        }
        relationshipStudents[studentKey].basic_info.is_in_team = false;


        applyGameDataToMvuContainer(mvuData, gameData);
        await persistMvuGameData(mvuData);

        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.success('学生已离队');
        }

        currentPhoneData = gameData;
        window.mvuGameData = gameData;
        const content = generateTeamPanel(gameData);
        $('#phone-app-body').html(content);
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                loadTeamStudentImages();
            });
        });

    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error('移除失败: ' + error.message);
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 出发前往处理事件
 */
async function departForEvent(eventKey) {

    const worldInfo = currentPhoneData?.world_info || {};
    const events = worldInfo.events || {};
    const event = events[eventKey];

    if (!event) {
        return;
    }

    const eventName = event.name || eventKey;
    const message = `出发前往处理"${restoreEraText(eventName)}"事件`;

    // 使用 MessageSender 发送消息到酒馆
    try {
        if (!window.messageSender) {
            throw new Error('消息发送器未初始化');
        }

        const success = await window.messageSender.sendToChat(message);

        if (success) {
            if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
                toastr.success('消息已发送: ' + message);
            }

            // 返回到新闻列表
            goBack();
        } else {
            throw new Error('发送失败');
        }
    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error('发送消息失败: ' + error.message);
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 删除事件
 */
async function deleteEvent(eventKey) {

    const worldInfo = currentPhoneData?.world_info || {};
    const events = worldInfo.events || {};
    const event = events[eventKey];

    if (!event) {
        return;
    }

    const eventName = restoreEraText(event.name || eventKey);

    // 显示确认对话框（使用Promise方式）
    const confirmed = await showCustomConfirm({
        title: '删除事件',
        message: `确定要删除事件"${eventName}"吗？<br><br>删除后该事件将从列表中移除。`,
        icon: '',
        confirmText: '确认删除',
        cancelText: '取消'
    });

    if (!confirmed) {
        return;
    }

    // 确认删除
    try {

        const mvuData = fetchRawMvuData();
        const gameData = extractMvuGameData(mvuData);

        if (!gameData.world_info || !gameData.world_info.events) {
            throw new Error('未找到事件数据');
        }

        // 检查事件是否存在
        if (!gameData.world_info.events[eventKey]) {
            throw new Error('事件不存在');
        }

        //  直接删除事件
        delete gameData.world_info.events[eventKey];

        applyGameDataToMvuContainer(mvuData, gameData);
        await persistMvuGameData(mvuData);

        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.success('事件已删除');
        }

        //  立即刷新数据并返回到新闻列表
        currentPhoneData = gameData;

        // 返回到新闻列表
        if (navigationStack.length > 0) {
            goBack();
            // 返回后立即刷新内容
            setTimeout(() => {
                const content = generateNewsPanel(gameData);
                $('#phone-app-body').html(content);
            }, 50);
        } else {
            // 如果栈为空，直接刷新当前页面
            const content = generateNewsPanel(gameData);
            $('#phone-app-body').html(content);
        }

    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error('删除失败: ' + error.message);
        }
    }
}

// ==================== 任务相关函数 ====================

/**
 * 放弃任务功能
 */
async function abandonTask(taskKey) {

    try {
        // 获取聊天变量
        const mvuData = fetchRawMvuData();
        const gameData = extractMvuGameData(mvuData);

        if (!gameData || !gameData.protagonist) {
            throw new Error('无法获取游戏数据');
        }

        const protagonist = gameData.protagonist || {};
        const quest = protagonist.quest || {};
        const active = quest.active || {};

        // 检查任务是否存在
        if (!active[taskKey]) {
            if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
                toastr.warning('任务不存在或已被删除');
            }
            return;
        }

        const taskData = active[taskKey];

        // 从进行中列表删除任务
        delete active[taskKey];

        // 更新MVU数据结构
        quest.active = active;
        protagonist.quest = quest;
        gameData.protagonist = protagonist;

        applyGameDataToMvuContainer(mvuData, gameData);
        await persistMvuGameData(mvuData);


        // 显示成功提示
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.success(`已放弃并删除任务：${taskData.title || taskKey}`, '删除成功');
        }

        // 刷新任务面板
        setTimeout(() => {
            const latestGameData = refreshPhoneData();
            if (latestGameData && latestGameData.protagonist) {
                currentPhoneData = latestGameData;
                const content = generateTasksPanel(latestGameData);
                $('#phone-app-body').html(content);
            }
        }, 500);

    } catch (error) {
        if (typeof toastr !== 'undefined') {
            toastr.error(`放弃任务失败: ${error.message}`, '错误');
        }
    }
}

// ==================== 启动 ====================
$(() => {
    initializeMobilePhone();
});

// ESC键关闭手机或全屏查看器
$(document).on('keydown', function (e) {
    if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        // 优先关闭全屏壁纸查看器
        const $viewer = $('#wallpaper-fullscreen-viewer');
        if ($viewer.hasClass('active')) {
            closeWallpaperFullscreen();
            return;
        }

        // 然后关闭手机界面（如果未置顶）
        const overlay = $('#mobile-phone-overlay');
        if (overlay.hasClass('active') && !isPinned) {
            closeMobilePhone();
        }
    }
});

// 卸载时清理
$(window).on('unload', () => {
    cleanupMobilePhone();
});
